Hi Scar! Others may have pointed this out, but a couple of easy ways to fall-proof your base (without pouring water everywhere) are berry bushes and powdered snow. Both will eliminate fall damage from any height. Placing carpet over powdered snow will even prevent you from sinking into it or taking cold damage. :)

Just wanted to say that your axe got switched with your food into the off-hand slot because you probably pressed 'F'.
